Summary: Great Pizza, Higher on Price but quality is worth it, staff can be rude, delivery is excellent and driver is professional, delivery time is fast, and food tastes good and arrives hot.

As for the food, the quality of round table speaks for itself. This review is more about this particular restaurant. I prefer to order from here rather than the one on Mary Ave. The food is always hot, prices are high but that's Round Table. Also, I noted the person taking calls today was rather indifferent/less friendly than others I've dealt with. So taking a star off for that one.

Otherwise, the delivery is superb here. The driver has come here three times already and is always polite, offers cheese and peppers, smiles, and makes it on time. So one of the main reasons I return here is for the food quality and delivery experience. If the order taking is unpleasant again, I may switch to online ordering.

In summary, one of the better round tables in the area.<//Text>

I made an order this evening after finding your shop on Google. The hours on Google were listed as closing at 10:00pm, and I made my order through the Round Table website at 8:40pm. I entered the shop and told the employee that I was there to pick up my pizza he said "You know we're closed, right?" < Text>
Very friendly guys, good attitude. The drawback was the spots that were missed. When I'd ask if they'd go try two certain spots, they willing did and the report came back that the spots came right out. The spots were pretty obvious in the room.My carpet is all one color. Why didn't they get it in the first place?  They were already down the hall and into the last bedroom. Same with the dirt trail from the kitchen to the hall. I mentioned that the carpet came clean just 8 (but it was 11) months earlier when they came. They ran over the spot and-Waa Laa- it came out perfect. I had my couch cleaned at this same time....when they had me check for satisfaction, there was the soiled spots on the cushion I had pointed out at the very beginning which was why they were here in the first place. They went over it (and the whole cushion) and it's brilliant. So the job got done perfectly but I had to bring them back to troubling spots.
In case you think they used extra measures to make it happen, there was no bottles of spot remover used, they didn't say it was a tough stain-in fact "it came right out!" was the quote, and the spot wasn't hidden or unseen. The wand had gone over the whole area previously.
With all that said, they are the best carpet and couch cleaners in Fresno so far. When they ask you to check the room they just finished, do it so you are happy with the results. Call them, Both times I've used them I was happy with the results and it was worth the money.
PS- the 1st time I had Stanley Steamer come, they got everything the first time. Maybe it's the truck.... don't be afraid to ask for a re-do on a spot.< /Text>

<Name>Victoria P.<//Name>< time>
1417499367373</time>
<Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
I went here for happy hour with my roommate before we went off to our respective events.  The happy hour menu is an extensive one compared to other menus I've seen at sushi restaurants.  And the prices were really good too.

I ordered the crunchy cannon roll, which was $6 (normally $8).  It was really delicious!  It was fried to perfection, and the honey mustard and unagi glaze gave it sweetness.  I can predict that some people might find this signature roll too sweet, but I enjoyed it.  What I also like was that they didn't skimp on the portion.  I got about 10 pieces, which didn't make me full, especially since I also ordered ahi poke.  Which, btw, was also very good.  It came with wontons, and added a salty flavor to this acidic dish.

The atmosphere is dark, and it can get loud inside.  The wait staff are really friendly and are happy to answer any questions you have.

I would definitely come back here and take advantage of their happy hour menu.  You get the best of what they offer at a good price, especially for the Marina.< /Review>

<Pics>None</Pics><gmap_id>0x808580d721a16de1:0x7365968bb36203d9<//gmap_id><user_name>Catherine Chang</user_name><UserId.>118373223335675400587<//UserId.><Resp>None<//Resp><Review>Your average sushi restaurant, but it does have some relatively good deals during happy hour.  We dropped in after the Union Street Festival for something light and relatively low-key, and that is exactly what we got.

During happy hour, the fancier rolls (i.e. sunset roll, rainbow rolls, etc.) are 25% off, small rolls (i.e. tuna roll, hamachi roll, etc.) are $3.00 , nigiri  is $1.50, and hand rolls are $2.00.

I don't really have any rolls to recommend, since none really impressed me. The rolls are small, the fish mediocre, and I felt like the rice was not pressed tightly enough when they made the rolls. The sun set strip we ordered, which is a roll consisted of tuna, yellowtail, minced salmon, and avocado wrapped in cucumber with no rice and soaked in vinegar was disappointing. It came with only 4 pieces and one of the pieces was missing avocado, again, demonstrating the sushi chef's lack of focus and precision.  I did, however, enjoy the spicy scallop hand roll, but it was pretty standard and nothing to get excited about either.

The service here is a bit under par. The waitresses were not rude, but they also didn't pay a whole lot of attention to our table.

All in all, it was not a terrible experience, but nothing here compels me to return again.</Review><Date>1383157185928<//Date>< Rate>

< text>
Wursthaus is my go-to bar! The best thing about this place is the happy hour. On Sundays, there's happy hour all day! Also, downtown Santa Ana has free parking on Sundays so it's a double win! I always order the Paulaner. I love that beer so much that sometimes I crave it and during happy hour, it only costs 4 dollars for 16 ounces!!

The bar itself is really amazing with 20 beers on tap with a large variety. Even if you're not a huge beer drinker there's probably a drink here for you! On top of the great prices, good beer and large variety, the food is also amazing! If you like onions, get the drunk fries! The onions are caramelized in IPA so it has a sweet taste! Definitely a place to check out!</text>

ocated off 4th street in Santa Ana next to the Frida Theater. At first you'd think as you walk in this place is a take out place. Once you order you meal you walk down the hall to the back where there are tables and a bar. It's really loud with music and people talking over the music. It's dark too. They bring your order to you. It's actually similar to Doghaus in terms of ordering at the counter getting a number and they bringing your order. I was very basic on mine I just got the nurnberger and bun since that was one of the non spicy ones and no toppings or anything it was not bad it was tasty. Overall not a bad place just not my cup of tea on the selections.</Review>

<user>114282066999760495988< /user>< user_name>
Craig Honorof< /user_name>
<Date>1559581944458</Date><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
I have been to many places that serve beer or serve brats but this place serves both!  I ordered a Polish sausage and an order of fries.  This came out to a little bit over $12 and change.  Not too bad but a little on the pricey side.  I went further into the place and found a seat.  The place was quite dark but I located my party.  The food came and the first thing I noticed was the bun to dog ratio was off (too much bun to dog) I had ordered it with raw onion (there was a grilled onion version too) and they were plentiful and sweet.  There was mustard on the table so I added it too.  After making my way through the considerable bun I hit pay dirt!  The dog was very tasty and well worth the wait.  Hot and savory with a hint of spice.  The mustard was great counter point with the dog still holding its own in the flavors amongst the crunchiness and sweetness of the onions.  Before I new it, it was gone.  Hmm sad but a happy moment too. On to the fries.  They were hot and aplenty. They had just been made and were very good.  Sweet and salty - no ketchup needed.  I also ordered an iced tea (didn't feel like a beer) and it came in a bottle.  Not a normal brand but still good.  Take a moment out of your busy schedule and do yourself a favor stop in for a treat!<//Review>

<review>Can't beat this place to fuel up with some knockwurst and beer.  If you have 30 mins before (or after) a film at The Frida Cinema (or anywhere else in downtown Santa Ana) then this is a great spot to replenish.

It is a good place for groups to meet up.

Great, wide range of German beers.  Every beer has its own custom glass.  Pay attention, they range from 8 to 16 ounces, and the range in flavor is big too.

But "late night"?   10pm is about the latest.  That's when they'll be trying to shut down the food and the bar will actually stop serving beer very soon after that.  So, you can only depend the Wursthaus until 10pm even on weekends.<//review><rating>4< /rating></record></dataset><record>

< user_name>
MrMoruss78 Mo</user_name>

1524028055370<//Date>
< rate>
4< /rate>
< review>
If you're into Brats this is your place to be in Santa Ana.  If you're into wild game meats, transformed into sausages, this is your place to be. If you're into German or European beers, come here.

Waking in the front door, the place looks like cozy and quaint. But wait, it ain't.  After ordering food at the front, the hallway to your right leads to where the real magic is.  Das beer. And here, they Steve Das Boot! Yes you heard it right, Das Boot just like in the movie BeerFest.  Now there are certain rules to ordering Das Boot; those of which you can read at the Wursthaus.

Myself, I ordered a Gulden Drak, my compadre ordered a double chocolate Stout, asks my other buddy ordered a Spaten and a wild boar bratwurst.

It was as simple as 1,2,3. Order food, order beer, sit down and eat.

Come to this place and get your WURST on.< /review>

<rating>4</rating><Text>Discovered this place while out with a friend checking out the new 4th Street Market nearby. She mentioned it was open super late - like until 4am and I made a mental note to suggest this spot to the boy because we're always looking for places to hang out late and drink.

California law says you can only serve alcohol until 2AM and you can only drink until 2AM in a public place so meh. Not sure how that's going to play out for these boys. However the spot is really cool even tho it's a bit of a hassle if you want to eat.

Upon entering it's a bit confusing. The food ordering process is front and center. Skip that and just head back if you want to drink. That's where it's dark and communal but we wanted no part of that so we headed to the bar and luckily found a quiet spot in the back with the bartender's complete attention for drinks and got our drink on. Boy felt like fries so we learned the hard way that you had to close the tab, go place an order and then come back. Bartender was cool enough to save our awesome seats and luckily you don't have to wait around for the food. You can order and they'll bring it.

Fries were good. Very potatoey with a choice of 3 dipping sauces. I do like my dipping sauces and they go beyond just standard ranch.

Overall, we really liked the place and vibe. It made for a good Friday and week ending. We both needed to de-stress and this was just awesome.<//Text></record></dataset><record>
